 In a meeting with students of the Moscow State Institute of International Relations, Russian Foreign Minister Sergei Lavrov said that the current problem of territorial disputes and the peace agreement between Russia and Japan would not be resolved under the APEC draft, according to Xinhua
 lavarove ne shanivaar ko kaha, "apek main kisi bhi antaraji, raajnneetik yaa kanoonee vyavasthaaon par vichaar nahin kiya jayega
 "he said that this 21-member regional organization has been functioning as a platform of economic dialogue since its inception
 tippaniyan Due to this territorial dispute between the two countries, the peace agreement between the two countries has been blocked since the Second World War
 lavarove ne haalanki vidhyaarthiyon se kaha ki shanti samjhaute kii anupasthiti se rus-japan ke bich dwipaksheeya sambandhon kaa vikaas prabhavit nahin hoga
 The APEC summit is held from 2 September to 9 September
 rus or japan ke bich lambe samay se prashanth ke chaar vivaadit dwipon kii samprabhutaa ko lekar vivaad chal rahaa he
